<div style="width:0;height:0;clear:both"></div><dl class="lemmaWgt-lemmaTitle lemmaWgt-lemmaTitle-">
<dd class="lemmaWgt-lemmaTitle-title">
<span class="lemma-pinyin">
<span class="text">[zhū bā jiè]</span>
<a class="speak" href="javascript:;" id="j-pinyin-speak" nslog-type="10000106" title="点击发声"> </a>
</span>
<div id="fmp_flash_div" style="position:absolute; left:-9999px;">
<audio id="audio" src=""></audio>
</div>
<h1>猪八戒</h1>
<h2>（中国神话小说《西游记》的角色）</h2>
<a class="edit-lemma cmn-btn-hover-blue cmn-btn-28 j-edit-link" href="javascript:;"><em class="cmn-icon wiki-lemma-icons wiki-lemma-icons_edit-lemma"></em>编辑</a>
<a class="lock-lemma" href="/view/10812319.htm" target="_blank" title="锁定"><em class="cmn-icon wiki-lemma-icons wiki-lemma-icons_lock-lemma"></em>锁定</a>
</dd>
</dl><div class="promotion-declaration">
</div><div class="lemma-summary" label-module="lemmaSummary">
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒是明朝<a data-lemmaid="6658261" href="/item/%E5%B0%8F%E8%AF%B4%E5%AE%B6/6658261" target="_blank">小说家</a><a data-lemmaid="74708" href="/item/%E5%90%B4%E6%89%BF%E6%81%A9/74708" target="_blank">吴承恩</a>所作《<a href="/item/%E8%A5%BF%E6%B8%B8%E8%AE%B0" target="_blank">西游记</a>》中登场的虚拟角色。又名<a href="/item/%E7%8C%AA%E5%88%9A%E9%AC%A3" target="_blank">猪刚鬣</a>，法号悟能，浑名<a data-lemmaid="3680243" href="/item/%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/3680243" target="_blank">八戒</a>，是<a href="/item/%E5%94%90%E5%83%A7" target="_blank">唐僧</a>的二徒弟，会天罡数的三十六般变化，所持武器为<a data-lemmaid="53988" href="/item/%E5%A4%AA%E4%B8%8A%E8%80%81%E5%90%9B/53988" target="_blank">太上老君</a>所造、玉皇大帝亲赐的上宝沁金钯（俗称九齿钉耙）。猪八戒前世为执掌天河八万水军的<a data-lemmaid="5216" href="/item/%E5%A4%A9%E8%93%AC%E5%85%83%E5%B8%85/5216" target="_blank">天蓬元帅</a>，一直倾慕容貌过人的霓裳仙子（属于<a data-lemmaid="68389" href="/item/%E5%AB%A6%E5%A8%A5/68389" target="_blank">嫦娥</a>中的一员，《西游记》中“嫦娥”是对月府所有仙女的称呼。并非民间传说里的羿妻姮娥）。《西游记》中各路神仙基本借鉴了正统<a href="/item/%E9%81%93%E6%95%99" target="_blank">道教</a>神仙录，由<a data-lemmaid="50934" href="/item/%E9%AB%98%E8%80%81%E5%BA%84/50934" target="_blank">高老庄</a>一集猪八戒提及可见，猪八戒的前世天蓬元帅即是水神天河宪节。</div><div class="para" label-module="para">因调戏霓裳仙子并且惹来纠察灵官后，又拱倒<a href="/item/%E6%96%97%E7%89%9B%E5%AE%AB" target="_blank">斗牛宫</a>被贬下凡尘，却又错投猪胎，后受观音点化，成为<a data-lemmaid="338052" href="/item/%E5%94%90%E5%83%A7/338052" target="_blank">唐僧</a>的弟子，与孙悟空一同保护唐僧去西天取经，最后被封为<a href="/item/%E5%87%80%E5%9D%9B%E4%BD%BF%E8%80%85" target="_blank">净坛使者</a>。</div>
</div>
<div class="configModuleBanner">

<a class="lemma-anchor " name="hotspotmining"></a>
</div><ul class="hotspotminingNavbar clearfix">
<li class="active" data-id="235395">TA说</li>
</ul>
<div class="hotspotminingContent clearfix showPic" id="hotspotminingContent-235395" style="display: block">
<div class="hotspotminingContent_pic ">
<a href="https://baike.baidu.com/tashuo/browse/content?id=76f8efb940c1c8cf8ffed6a5&amp;fr=qingtian&amp;lemmaId=769" target="_blank"><img src="https://gss1.bdstatic.com/-vo3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/whfpf%3D180%2C140%2C50/sign=2e8e252f73f0f736d8ab1f416c688221/fc1f4134970a304ea0f5b3aadac8a786c8175c8e.jpg"/></a>
</div>
<div class="hotspotminingContent_cnt ">
<div class="hotspotminingContent_cnt_tit"><span class="hotspotminingContent_cnt_tit_tit"><a href="https://baike.baidu.com/tashuo/browse/content?id=76f8efb940c1c8cf8ffed6a5&amp;fr=qingtian&amp;lemmaId=769" target="_blank">西游记中最被轻视的人，看似胆小怕事，关键时刻却多次救了悟空</a></span><img src="https://bkssl.bdimg.com/static/wiki-lemma/widget/lemma_content/configModule/hotspotmining/img/flag_new_c80aa2a.png"/>
<span class="hotspotminingContent_cnt_tit_tim">2017-10-21 18:10</span>
</div>
<div class="hotspotminingContent_cnt_cnt">
<span>西游记里不乏聪明的主，不过要说起大智若愚者，他们都排不上号。诸位可能想说，那还有谁，难道是唐僧？非也，一个遇事毫无主见只会念阿弥陀佛的主，谈何大智若愚。沙和尚更不是，碰到困难就会一句话: 大师兄快来，师傅不见了！难不成是蠢头蠢脑的猪八戒？对，恭喜你猜对了，曾经的天蓬元帅猪悟能，他才是整部西游记里最聪明的，只不过一直都在装糊涂罢了。</span><a href="https://baike.baidu.com/tashuo/browse/content?id=76f8efb940c1c8cf8ffed6a5&amp;fr=qingtian&amp;lemmaId=769" target="_blank">...详情</a></div>
</div>

<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="1"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_1"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="人物介绍"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-2" label-module="para-title">
<h2 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>人物介绍</h2>
<a class="edit-icon j-edit-link" data-edit-dl="1" href="javascript:;"><em class="cmn-icon wiki-lemma-icons wiki-lemma-icons_edit-lemma"></em>编辑</a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><a class="lemma-album layout-right nslog:10000206" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/16674007/b03533fa828ba61e82d57e044534970a304e59e5?fr=lemma&amp;ct=cover" nslog-type="10000206" style="width:148px;" target="_blank" title="猪八戒">
<div class="album-wrap" style="width:146px;height:220px;">
<img alt="猪八戒" class="picture" src="https://gss2.bdstatic.com/9fo3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=51ead7fc32d12f2eca05a9627fc2d5ff/b03533fa828ba61e82d57e044534970a304e59e5.jpg" style="width:146px;height:220px;"/>
</div>
<div class="description">
猪八戒<span class="number">(7张)</span>
</div>
<div class="albumBg">
<div class="albumBgFir" style="width:140px;"></div>
<div class="albumBgSec" style="width:134px;"></div>
</div>
</a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">原是天庭<a href="/item/%E7%8E%89%E7%9A%87%E5%A4%A7%E5%B8%9D" target="_blank">玉皇大帝</a>手下的<a data-lemmaid="5216" href="/item/%E5%A4%A9%E8%93%AC%E5%85%83%E5%B8%85/5216" target="_blank">天蓬元帅</a>，主管天河。后因喝醉酒调戏霓裳仙子并大声喧哗惹来纠察灵官，而后又一嘴拱倒<a href="/item/%E6%96%97%E7%89%9B%E5%AE%AB" target="_blank">斗牛宫</a>并偷吃了灵芝仙草被<a href="/item/%E7%8E%89%E7%9A%87%E5%A4%A7%E5%B8%9D" target="_blank">玉皇大帝</a>责令两千余锤后贬下凡间。到人间投胎，却错投猪胎，嘴脸与野猪相似，曾占<a href="/item/%E7%A6%8F%E9%99%B5%E5%B1%B1" target="_blank">福陵山</a>云栈洞为妖。它<a href="/item/%E5%92%AC%E6%9D%80" target="_blank">咬杀</a>母猪，打死群彘，又招赘到福陵山<a href="/item/%E4%BA%91%E6%A0%88%E6%B4%9E" target="_blank">云栈洞</a>的卵二姐（说法其一：卵这个字用在名字上，含有一定的荤段子意味；说法其二：“卵”实则为“卯”，据考证卯二姐原型应是兔子精），想不到一年后卵二姐却死了，只留下一个洞府给他。至此栖身云栈洞，自称“<a href="/item/%E7%8C%AA%E5%88%9A%E9%AC%A3" target="_blank">猪刚鬣</a>”。<a href="/item/%E5%94%90%E5%83%A7" target="_blank">唐僧</a>西去取经路过高老庄，在云栈洞与<a data-lemmaid="5576" href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E6%82%9F%E7%A9%BA/5576" target="_blank">孙悟空</a>大战，听说唐僧之名，前去拜见。被唐僧收为二徒弟后，为让其继续戒五荤三厌，唐僧给他起了个别名叫“八戒”。八戒从此成为<a href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E6%82%9F%E7%A9%BA" target="_blank">孙悟空</a>的好帮手，一同保护唐僧去西天取经。<sup>[1]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[1]_5039852"> </a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">在《<a href="/item/%E8%A5%BF%E6%B8%B8%E8%AE%B0%E5%89%8D%E4%BC%A0" target="_blank">西游记前传</a>》中介绍了猪八戒被封为天蓬元帅和被贬下界的背景缘由。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">在小说当中，由于他的懒惰、贪吃和好色，常常使唐僧师徒陷于困境当中。取回真经后，猪八戒由于“又有顽心，色性未泯”被封为<a href="/item/%E5%87%80%E5%9D%9B%E4%BD%BF%E8%80%85" target="_blank">净坛使者</a>。会三十六变，能腾云驾雾，使用的兵器是九齿钉钯，又叫上宝沁金钯。在《<a href="/item/%E8%A5%BF%E6%B8%B8%E8%AE%B0" target="_blank">西游记</a>》中，猪八戒也称木母或木龙（猪八戒属真阴，<a href="/item/%E4%BA%94%E8%A1%8C" target="_blank">五行</a>属木），常见于目录或书中诗赋。<sup>[2]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[2]_5039852"> </a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">注：第61回“猪八戒助力败魔王”中，猪八戒自己也作了一首诗说：“木生在亥配为猪，牵转牛儿归土类。申下生金却是猴，无刑无克多和气。用芭蕉，为水意，焰火消除成既济。昼夜休离苦尽功，功完赶赴盂兰会。”<sup>[3]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[3]_5039852"> </a>
<a name="ref_3"></a><a name="ref_3"></a><a name="ref_3"></a></div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="1_1"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_1_1"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="姓名来历"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="1-1"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>姓名来历</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒以相为姓，唤名猪刚鬣。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">《西游记》中猪刚鬣受了菩萨戒行，断了<a href="/item/%E4%BA%94%E8%8D%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%8E%8C" target="_blank">五荤三厌</a>，唐僧因此给他起了个，叫做“八戒”。五荤三厌属宗教戒条，信徒不准食用。 五荤，即<a href="/item/%E4%BA%94%E8%BE%9B" target="_blank">五辛</a>，指五种辛味蔬菜。包括大蒜、小葱、韭与渠（形似萝卜味如蒜）。三厌，道教把雁、狗、乌龟作为不能吃的三种动物，列为教条。认为“雁有夫妇之伦，狗有扈主之谊；乌龟有君臣忠敬之心，故不忍食”（《<a href="/item/%E6%B6%8C%E5%B9%A2%E5%B0%8F%E5%93%81" target="_blank">涌幢小品</a>》）。厌，在此是不忍食之意。不过，这五荤三厌是佛道二教的混合物，佛教的“八戒”实际另有所指。 八戒全称“八斋戒”，是佛教为出家的男女教徒制定的八项戒条。包括不杀生，不偷盗，不淫欲，不妄语，不饮酒，不眠坐华丽之床，不打扮及观听歌舞，正午过后不食。佛教戒律还有很多。猪悟能虽称“八戒”，但他始终“戒”得不彻底，也不情愿。 唐僧给八戒取的名字是有一定含义的。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="1_2"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_1_2"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="性格特点"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="1-2"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>性格特点</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:220px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/cb8065380cd79123dd07b6bfa4345982b3b78011?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:220px;height:154px;" target="_blank" title="">
<img alt="" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss2.bdstatic.com/9fo3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=27f858b129a446237acaa260a8207246/cb8065380cd79123dd07b6bfa4345982b3b78011.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:220px;height:154px;"/>
</a>
</div>猪八戒性格憨厚，力气大，但好吃懒做，胆小，爱占小便宜，贪图女色，经常被妖怪的美色所迷惑，难分敌我。猪八戒贪吃贪睡，好进谗言。他常常想捉弄人，但不是搬起石头来砸自己的脚就是作茧自缚。为什么连这样一个人也最终修成正果，被<a href="/item/%E5%A6%82%E6%9D%A5%E4%BD%9B" target="_blank">如来佛</a>封为“<a href="/item/%E5%87%80%E5%9D%9B%E4%BD%BF%E8%80%85" target="_blank">净坛使者</a>”。这与猪八戒的知错就改，能听取他人意见有重要联系（其实这与悟空的‘督促’有很大关系），做到了悬崖勒马、甚至是浪子回头。在取经事业中的他对师兄的话还算得上言听计从，对师父忠心耿耿，总算是为西天取经立下汗马功劳，才有净坛使者的美好结果吧。《西游记》是具有浓郁象征意味的神魔小说的代表作，而猪八戒则是作者吴承恩在这部作品中着力塑造的一个喜剧典型。在他的身上既有人的吃苦耐劳、憨厚率直的品质以及贪婪自私的本性，又有神的本领，同时还有猪的形体特征，这充分体现了作者把人性、神性、猪性的完美结合。<sup>[4]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[4]_5039852"> </a>
</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="1_3"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_1_3"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="外貌形象"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="1-3"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>外貌形象</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><b>外貌描写：</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">“黑脸短毛，长喙大耳，穿一身青不青，蓝不蓝的梭布直裰，系一条花布手巾。”这就是猪八戒的外在形象。<sup>[3]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[3]_5039852"> </a>
<a name="ref_3"></a><a name="ref_3"></a><a name="ref_3"></a></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">初来时，是一条黑胖汉，后来就变做一个长嘴大耳朵的呆子，脑后又有一溜<a href="/item/%E9%AC%83%E6%AF%9B" target="_blank">鬃毛</a>，身体粗糙怕人，头脸就象个猪的模样。食肠却又甚大，一顿要吃三五斗米饭。<sup>[5]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[5]_5039852"> </a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><b>诗词描写：</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">第八十五回：碓嘴初长三尺零，獠牙觜出赛银钉。一双圆眼光如电，两耳扇风唿唿声。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">脑后鬃长排铁箭，浑身皮糙癞还青。手中使件蹊跷物，九齿钉钯个个惊。<sup>[6]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[6]_5039852"> </a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">獠牙锋利如钢锉，长嘴张开似火盆。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">第八回：金盔紧系腮边带，勒甲丝绦蟒退鳞。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">手执钉耙龙探爪，腰挎弯弓月半轮。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">纠纠威风欺太岁，昂昂志气压天神。<sup>[7]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[7]_5039852"> </a>
</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="1_4"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_1_4"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="角色原型"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="1-4"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>角色原型</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><i>猪八戒原型</i><sup>[8]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[8]_5039852"> </a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:117px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/0824ab18972bd407158d5d237d899e510eb309a1?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:117px;height:220px;" target="_blank" title="净坛使者-猪八戒">
<img alt="净坛使者-猪八戒" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss0.bdstatic.com/94o3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=138d3965a01ea8d38e227306a70b30cf/0824ab18972bd407158d5d237d899e510eb309a1.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:117px;height:220px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
净坛使者-猪八戒
</span>
</div><a data-lemmaid="36231" href="/item/%E9%B2%81%E8%BF%85/36231" target="_blank">鲁迅</a>认为猪八戒的形象是从中国古代神话传说中发展演变而来，例如<a href="/item/%E5%B9%B2%E5%AE%9D" target="_blank">干宝</a>《<a href="/item/%E6%90%9C%E7%A5%9E%E8%AE%B0" target="_blank">搜神记</a>》“猪臂金铃”故事，旷源《闲话猪八戒》一文补充了鲁迅的论点，他认为《<a href="/item/%E6%90%9C%E7%A5%9E%E8%AE%B0" target="_blank">搜神记</a>》“安阳亭书生”中母猪精更接近猪八戒。<a href="/item/%E5%90%B4%E8%87%AA%E7%89%A7" target="_blank">吴自牧</a>《梦梁录》曾提到“天蓬”本为道教仙官门。<a href="/item/%E9%99%88%E5%AF%85%E6%81%AA" target="_blank">陈寅恪</a>《西游记玄奘弟子故事之演变》一文推考猪八戒是从唐义净译《<a href="/item/%E6%A0%B9%E6%9C%AC%E8%AF%B4%E4%B8%80%E5%88%87%E6%9C%89%E9%83%A8%E6%AF%97%E5%A5%88%E8%80%B6%E6%9D%82%E4%BA%8B" target="_blank">根本说一切有部毗奈耶杂事</a>》卷三《佛制苾刍发不应长因缘》中变大猪救沙门之大神衍化而成的。陈寅恪又说：“猪八戒高家庄招亲故事，必非全出中国人臆撰，而印度又无猪豕招亲之事……此故事复经后来之讲说，闪毗国之，以音相同之故，变为高家庄之高。惊犯宫女，以事相类似之故，变为招亲”。<sup>[9]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[9]_5039852"> </a>
</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="1_5"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_1_5"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="身世来历"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="1-5"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>身世来历</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:145px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/e824b899a9014c087cff18bf0d7b02087af4f4e7?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:145px;height:220px;" target="_blank" title="葛民辉版猪八戒">
<img alt="葛民辉版猪八戒" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss2.bdstatic.com/9fo3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=bfb2d43974f082022992963d7bfafb8a/e824b899a9014c087cff18bf0d7b02087af4f4e7.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:145px;height:220px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
葛民辉版猪八戒
</span>
</div>根据《西游记》故事，猪八戒原是天庭中统领八万天河水兵的天蓬元帅，由于<a href="/item/%E8%9F%A0%E6%A1%83%E4%BC%9A" target="_blank">蟠桃会</a>上喝酒醉后调戏月宫的霓裳仙子，打了两千锤后被贬下凡，又投错胎变成猪模样，入赘高老庄。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">自小生来心性拙，贪闲爱懒无休歇。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">不曾养性与修真，混沌迷心熬日月。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">忽然闲里遇真仙，就把寒温坐下说。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">听言意转要修行，闻语心回求妙诀。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">有缘立地拜为师，指示天关并地阙。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">得传九转大还丹，工夫昼夜无时辍。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">三花聚顶得归根，五气朝元通透彻。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">功圆形满却飞升，天仙对对来迎接。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">敕封元帅管天河，总督水兵称宪节。<sup>[3]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[3]_5039852"> </a>
<a name="ref_3"></a><a name="ref_3"></a><a name="ref_3"></a></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">疑点：猪八戒说自己错投猪胎，其实是为了要面子，掩盖真相。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">第八十五回：巨口獠牙神力大，玉皇升我天蓬帅。掌管天河八万兵，天宫快乐多自在。只因酒醉戏宫娥，那时就把英雄卖。一嘴拱倒斗牛宫，吃了王母灵芝菜。玉皇亲打二千锤，把吾贬下三天界。教吾立志养元神，下方却又为妖怪。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">“巨口獠牙”、“一嘴拱倒”等说明猪八戒以前就是猪修成人形的，只是后来被玉皇打了二千锤，大伤元气和修为，又变回了猪样。直接从天上贬到了野猪窝里。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">这样就说清楚了几个疑点了，猪八戒“投胎”后有“前世”的记忆，一生下来就能咬死母猪及猪群，一生下来就会三十六变，还携带了九齿钉耙。“一嘴拱倒斗牛宫”说明当初的天蓬确实很厉害，斗牛宫是二十八宿的地盘，可是后来二十八宿之一的奎木狼（即：黄袍怪），猪八戒都已打不过，说明其修为被玉皇打了二千锤后，已经大减，而当初能做天蓬元帅确实是有实力的。三十六天罡的变化和七十二地煞的变化本来是差不多的，但因八戒修为大减，故给人感觉有些弱。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="1_6"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_1_6"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="使用武器"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="1-6"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>使用武器</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><a href="/item/%E4%B9%9D%E9%BD%BF%E9%92%89%E8%80%99" target="_blank">九齿钉耙</a>为其武器，这九齿钉耙名为上宝逊金钯，重量有一藏之数，连柄五千零四十八斤，是由<a href="/item/%E5%A4%AA%E4%B8%8A%E8%80%81%E5%90%9B" target="_blank">太上老君</a>用神冰铁锤炼，借五方五帝、六丁六甲之力锻造而成。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><b>原著中有描写</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">这钯岂是凡间之物？你且听我道来：<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:180px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/0b7b02087bf40ad1878ecd52572c11dfa9ecce1d?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:180px;height:220px;" target="_blank" title="猪八戒">
<img alt="猪八戒" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss1.bdstatic.com/-vo3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=aeacc46cab64034f0bcdc5049fc27980/0b7b02087bf40ad1878ecd52572c11dfa9ecce1d.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:180px;height:220px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
猪八戒
</span>
</div></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">此是煅炼神冰铁，磨琢成工光皎洁。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">老君自己动钤锤，荧惑亲身添炭屑。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">五方五帝用心机，六丁六甲费周折。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">造成九齿玉垂牙，铸就双环金坠叶。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">身妆六曜排五星，体按四时依八节。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">短长上下定乾坤，左右阴阳分日月。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">六爻神将按天条，八卦星辰依斗列。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">名为上宝逊金钯，进与玉皇镇丹阙。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">因我修成大罗仙，为吾养就长生客。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">敕封元帅号天蓬，钦赐钉钯为御节。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">举起烈焰并毫光，落下猛风飘瑞雪。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">天曹神将尽皆惊，地府阎罗心胆怯。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:149px; margin: 0px auto 0px 0px; clear: both; display: inline; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/c8177f3e6709c93de04615709f3df8dcd0005484?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:149px;height:220px;" target="_blank" title="崔景富版猪八戒">
<img alt="崔景富版猪八戒" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss0.bdstatic.com/94o3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=3766e0ac9d16fdfadc6cc1ec848e8cea/c8177f3e6709c93de04615709f3df8dcd0005484.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:149px;height:220px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
崔景富版猪八戒
</span>
</div></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">人间那有这般兵，世上更无此等铁。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">随身变化可心怀，任意翻腾依口诀。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">相携数载未曾离，伴我几年无日别。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">日食三餐并不丢，夜眠一宿浑无撇。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">也曾佩去赴蟠桃，也曾带他朝帝阙。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">皆因仗酒却行凶，只为倚强便撒泼。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">上天贬我降凡尘，下世尽我作罪孽。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">石洞心邪曾吃人，高庄情喜婚姻结。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">下海掀翻龙鼍窝，上山抓碎虎狼穴。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">诸般兵刃且休题，惟有吾当钯最切。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">相持取胜有何难，赌斗求功不用说。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">何怕你铜头铁脑一身钢，钯到魂消神气泄！<sup>[3]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[3]_5039852"> </a>
<a name="ref_3"></a><a name="ref_3"></a><a name="ref_3"></a></div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="2"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_2"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="形象意义"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-2" label-module="para-title">
<h2 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>形象意义</h2>
<a class="edit-icon j-edit-link" data-edit-dl="2" href="javascript:;"><em class="cmn-icon wiki-lemma-icons wiki-lemma-icons_edit-lemma"></em>编辑</a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒的形象具有时代意义。在《<a data-lemmaid="6786341" href="/item/%E8%A5%BF%E6%B8%B8%E8%AE%B0/6786341" target="_blank">西游记</a>》中，猪八戒不习惯更不喜欢长期在外奔波的苦行生活，他护僧取经是出于无奈的，在西行途中遇有劫难，总是第一个打退堂鼓，要散伙，卖行李、嚷着回高老庄做女婿、种地过日子，这种回归土地、眷念家园、渴望定居生活的心情，也正是长期依附于土地的典型的农民意识和农民心理。可以说，猪八戒是一个来自乡村的劳动人民的典型化身，他深刻存在守着土地而养成的顽固的保守心理，和神、<a data-lemmaid="2793631" href="/item/%E9%81%93/2793631" target="_blank">道</a>、<a href="/item/%E4%BD%9B" target="_blank">佛</a>相对立，表现着普通劳动人民的生活愿望。猪八戒身上贪财、贪色、自私自利，还表现着明代社会好色好货思想的沉淀，反映了当时小生产者、小市民的意识特点，具有那个时代的思想特色。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:220px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/2cf5e0fe9925bc314b19b7365edf8db1ca1370d3?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:220px;height:155px;" target="_blank" title="臧金生版猪八戒">
<img alt="臧金生版猪八戒" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss3.bdstatic.com/7Po3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=72418f49912397ddd2799f066983b216/2cf5e0fe9925bc314b19b7365edf8db1ca1370d3.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:220px;height:155px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
臧金生版猪八戒
</span>
</div>因为，随着明朝中叶商品经济的发展，中国新生的市民阶层继宋、元之后进一步壮大，并开始在社会中起着不可低估的作用。但由于中国已经衰落的封建经济仍然非常强大，整个社会仍然是自然经济占统治地位。所以，明朝新兴市民阶层中仍然存在着进步与保守两种因素。猪八戒的形象在明朝的市民阶层中具有普遍性，是个“充满人欲的艺术形象”，是中国传统社会生活中的一个代表着农民阶层并具有市民特征的下层人民形象。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒率性而为，张扬个性，其自然天性源于他是一个具有代表性的凡夫俗子；一个普普通通、安守本分，一个并不情愿、时时打退堂鼓地凡夫俗子；一个作为上至公卿下至百姓都可以轻松嘲笑并调侃的对象，一个来自于人民内部的、带有芸芸众生的人性优点及弱点的形象，因此，具有迎合大众文化的当代意义。如民间中的一些<a href="/item/%E6%AD%87%E5%90%8E%E8%AF%AD" target="_blank">歇后语</a>：“<a href="/item/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92%E8%83%8C%E5%AA%B3%E5%A6%87" target="_blank">猪八戒背媳妇</a>—费力不讨好”；“猪八戒耍耙子—就会一手”；“猪八戒掏耳朵—里面有货”当代也涌现出了几部关于猪八戒的影视产品，如《<a href="/item/%E6%98%A5%E5%85%89%E7%81%BF%E7%83%82%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92" target="_blank">春光灿烂猪八戒</a>》，《福星高照猪八戒》等。猪八戒之所以在当代大众文化圈里得到这样的欢迎，主要是与他的亲和力有关，与当今人们的精神需要有关。所以，在当代社会，猪八戒的形象是具有普遍意义的。<sup>[10]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[10]_5039852"> </a>
</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="3"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_3"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="作品意义"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-2" label-module="para-title">
<h2 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>作品意义</h2>
<a class="edit-icon j-edit-link" data-edit-dl="3" href="javascript:;"><em class="cmn-icon wiki-lemma-icons wiki-lemma-icons_edit-lemma"></em>编辑</a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">在作品中，这个人物与具有独特的思想意义和美学意义。<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:220px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/241f95cad1c8a7867637852b6609c93d70cf50f2?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:220px;height:165px;" target="_blank" title="央视动画版猪八戒">
<img alt="央视动画版猪八戒" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss3.bdstatic.com/7Po3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=5afd1d0491ef76c6d4d2fc29ad16fdf6/241f95cad1c8a7867637852b6609c93d70cf50f2.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:220px;height:165px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
央视动画版猪八戒
</span>
</div>他与<a href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E6%82%9F%E7%A9%BA" target="_blank">孙悟空</a>和<a href="/item/%E5%94%90%E5%83%A7" target="_blank">唐僧</a>各据三角形的一个角，构成了鲜明的对比，互相映衬，相得益彰。他与孙悟空都是用浪漫主义手法精心塑造出的非现实人物，正如谢肇浙所说，孙悟空是“意之神”，尽管他躁动不安，但总是在追求一种崇高的精神境界，其间难免走弯路，但只要加以引导制约，就能达到至高至纯的人生境界。而猪八戒则是“意之驰”，表现了对现实的生活享受的向往，安于现状，不求上进。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">两种心态，都不利于人生境界的提升。但与躁动的“心猿”相比，猪八戒身上常常体现出的消极情绪，更不利于人生境界的提升。因为前者毕竟是一种推动力，而后者则多是一种制动力。两者都基于传统文化的深厚土壤。孙悟空更多地体现了传统文化中的积极因素，如不畏艰险，勇往直前，不达目的决不罢休的气概，这种宗教献身主义精神是积极的，与传统文化中的积极人生理想是一致的，给人以昂扬向上的力量，因此他是一个英雄主义的角色。但猪八戒则较多地体现了传统文化中的消极因素。这是一个享乐主义的典型。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="4"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_4"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="相关作品"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-2" label-module="para-title">
<h2 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>相关作品</h2>
<a class="edit-icon j-edit-link" data-edit-dl="4" href="javascript:;"><em class="cmn-icon wiki-lemma-icons wiki-lemma-icons_edit-lemma"></em>编辑</a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">《<a href="/item/%E8%A5%BF%E6%B8%B8%E8%AE%B0%E5%89%8D%E4%BC%A0" target="_blank">西游记前传</a>》中介绍了猪八戒被封为天蓬元帅和被贬下界的幕后背景缘由。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="5"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_5"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="人物评价"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-2" label-module="para-title">
<h2 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>人物评价</h2>
<a class="edit-icon j-edit-link" data-edit-dl="5" href="javascript:;"><em class="cmn-icon wiki-lemma-icons wiki-lemma-icons_edit-lemma"></em>编辑</a>
</div>
<div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="5_1"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_5_1"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="整体评价"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="5-1"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>整体评价</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">凡事都有因果，对八戒的成才经验，总结出与他的名字有关系，也就是根据猪八戒的优点粗略统计一下，在各路的神仙领导、唐僧组长、孙悟空师兄、沙和尚师弟等方方面面，对八戒的及时监督和管理，猪八戒扎扎实实做出了八戒表现。八戒贪吃，险象环生。若不是悟空及时阻止，八戒早已成为群妖口中的美味。在“<a href="/item/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92%E5%90%83%E8%A5%BF%E7%93%9C" target="_blank">猪八戒吃西瓜</a>”这一段中他的特色最为突出。此乃戒贪吃，应该是八戒之一也。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><a class="lemma-album layout-right nslog:10000206" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/12319777/2f738bd4b31c8701b6ca7cc3267f9e2f0708ff93?fr=lemma&amp;ct=cover" nslog-type="10000206" style="width:171px;" target="_blank" title="谢宁版猪八戒">
<div class="album-wrap" style="width:169px;height:220px;">
<img alt="谢宁版猪八戒" class="picture" src="https://gss3.bdstatic.com/7Po3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=c346ceefe7cd7b89ed6c3d813f244291/2f738bd4b31c8701b6ca7cc3267f9e2f0708ff93.jpg" style="width:169px;height:220px;"/>
</div>
<div class="description">
谢宁版猪八戒<span class="number">(2张)</span>
</div>
<div class="albumBg">
<div class="albumBgFir" style="width:163px;"></div>
<div class="albumBgSec" style="width:157px;"></div>
</div>
</a>
八戒见到青年女子，总是心花怒放。多亏唐僧苦口婆心的教育，孙悟空、悟净的善意捉弄，才使其不良行为有所收敛。尤其是四位菩萨的精心点化，让八戒终生难忘。此乃戒贪色，应该是八戒之一也。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">取经路上每每遇到挫折困难，八戒总是惦记着私分悟净肩上的集体财物。悟空的痛打辱骂，悟净的挖苦谴责，才一次次打消了他分包袱的念头。此乃戒贪财，应该是八戒之一也。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">别看八戒对除妖降魔一筹莫展，但在领导面前打小报告却有一手。多亏唐僧心中有数，悟空、悟净的及时揭发谴责，才使八戒的阴谋一次次落空。此乃戒嫉贤，应该是八戒之一也。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">针对八戒的弄虚作假行为，悟空采取变化紧盯，跟踪偷袭的办法及时予以揭露和纠正，从而为唐僧正确决策提供详实的依据。戒做假，应该是八戒之一也。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">在<a href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E6%82%9F%E7%A9%BA" target="_blank">孙悟空</a>被赶走的这些时候里，它又因为贪睡，害得唐僧误入妖怪的洞穴。每逢八戒偷懒时，悟空要么变化对其捉弄以示警戒，要么以身作则吃苦在前，从而带动八戒积极工作。这样一来，弄得八戒心有余悸，不敢也不好意思再偷懒。此乃戒偷懒，应该是八戒之一也。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">遇到困难后当八戒打退堂鼓时，老是爱提各走各的路。唐僧、悟空、悟净都及时从 思想上予以助威鼓劲，从工作上为其排忧解难，激励八戒增强信心，心甘情愿的献身于取经事业。此乃戒畏难，应该是八戒之一也。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">对付八戒的贪功恶习，唐僧的做法是<a data-lemmaid="36312" href="/item/%E5%AE%9E%E4%BA%8B%E6%B1%82%E6%98%AF/36312" target="_blank">实事求是</a>，公开公正，论功行赏，悟空、悟净的态度是居功不傲，不卑不亢，<a data-lemmaid="71289" href="/item/%E5%BF%83%E5%B9%B3%E6%B0%94%E5%92%8C/71289" target="_blank">心平气和</a>。从而保证了取经队伍的团结一致。此乃戒贪功，应该是八戒之一也。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="5_2"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_5_2"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="优点"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="5-2"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>优点</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><b>心宽</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">做人一定要心宽。如果大事小事都管，处处斤斤计较，整天小肚鸡肠，那就很不好。这一点猪八戒可以说是楷模。唐僧师傅也深知，西天取经的路上，无论孙悟空怎么拿捏他，他从来就不计较。有好几回孙悟空掂着老猪的耳朵骂他是呆子是蠢货，人家老猪一回也没有生气过，依然是一口一个师兄地叫。遇到师傅师兄皆被妖怪擒走，<a href="/item/%E6%B2%99%E5%92%8C%E5%B0%9A" target="_blank">沙和尚</a>急的跳墙，老猪就不。你听人家老猪怎么说：急什么急，大不了散伙，俺回<a data-lemmaid="8513566" href="/item/%E9%AB%98%E8%80%81%E5%BA%84/8513566" target="_blank">高老庄</a>。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><b>老实</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">都说老实人可靠。但是，有人对这一点表示怀疑：去西天取经时，他就常常偷懒耍猾，有好几次孙悟空派他去打探妖情，他就玩忽职守，不干活只睡懒觉。对于这一点，组织上进行了严肃认真的考察和论证，最终得出的结论是：这样的认为有失偏颇。当时孙悟空是大师兄、是上司，<a href="/item/%E7%8B%AC%E6%96%AD%E4%B8%93%E8%A1%8C" target="_blank">独断专行</a>、<a href="/item/%E9%A3%9E%E6%89%AC%E8%B7%8B%E6%89%88" target="_blank">飞扬跋扈</a>是出了名的，玉皇大帝他也不怕，就是师傅，如果不是有那个金箍咒，他怎么可能把一个肉体凡胎的唐朝和尚放在眼里。孙悟空派他做什么，他一个小小的猪八戒还能怎么地，只有忍气吞声俯首贴耳一条路可走，别无他法。不过这也足以看出猪八戒之老实。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="5_3"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_5_3"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="缺点"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="5-3"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>缺点</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><b>贪吃</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">俗话说：民以食为天。当老百姓的都把吃放在第一，做为人更得把吃放在首位；要吃，一是要吃出道理；二是要吃出水平；三是要吃出自己的理念。猪八戒在这一方面就做的很优秀。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><b>懒做</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">这一点猪八戒更是优秀。能明天做的事今天绝对不做，能将来做的事一定不会立即做；要做也请别人去做，就说小事吧，有沙师弟在用得着猪师兄吗？如果是大事，只要有悟空大师兄在，猪八戒绝不会去抢师哥的功劳。西天取经的路上，沙僧和师傅等一旦被妖精拿住，别人都急得跳圈，唯八戒不急不躁，该吃的吃该喝的喝，当然前提是大师兄孙悟空不被擒获。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><b>贪睡</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><a href="/item/%E5%88%97%E5%AE%81" target="_blank">列宁</a>同志说：不会休息就不会工作。也就是说要想工作好就得休<a class="lemma-album layout-right nslog:10000206" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/2589466/962bd40735fae6cd9fcd60440eb30f2442a70f9e?fr=lemma&amp;ct=cover" nslog-type="10000206" style="width:155px;" target="_blank" title="猪八戒画像">
<div class="album-wrap" style="width:153px;height:220px;">
<img alt="猪八戒画像" class="picture" src="https://gss0.bdstatic.com/-4o3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=425a56c6fc1f4134e437027c151f95c1/962bd40735fae6cd9fcd60440eb30f2442a70f9e.jpg" style="width:153px;height:220px;"/>
</div>
<div class="description">
猪八戒画像<span class="number">(12张)</span>
</div>
<div class="albumBg">
<div class="albumBgFir" style="width:147px;"></div>
<div class="albumBgSec" style="width:141px;"></div>
</div>
</a>
息好，所以贪睡不是缺点。做人一定要学会睡觉，保证身体健康，就是保住了革命的本钱。有好多日理万机的领导干部，都是太不注意休息而累垮了身体，结果是留下一摊子未竟的事业，还得让别的特别懂得睡觉之道理的同志来完成。猪八戒贪睡是众所周知的，只要有机会睡，猪八戒同志认为那是不可不睡。有多少次师傅师兄委派他去打探妖情，他都会瞅机会好好地睡上一回，睡醒睡足睡够，回去编个理由便告万事大吉。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><b>体胖</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">人得有福像，一般要肥头大耳，不能瘦的跟干拉鸡似的。这一点唐僧师徒四人唯有猪八戒具备。去掉僧衣僧帽，换上西服打上领带，猪八戒走在大街上，谁敢说老猪不是领导。虽然猪八戒脸上一贯是和颜悦色，却也<a href="/item/%E4%B8%8D%E6%80%92%E8%87%AA%E5%A8%81" target="_blank">不怒自威</a>。不管什么时候只要老猪往前那么一站，再胆小的孩子也会吓得绝对不敢再哭；儿童尚且如此，妇女更是腿肚子发软，怎么也动不了步了。这就叫威严。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><b>好色</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:182px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/37d3d539b6003af366bd1645342ac65c1038b694?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:182px;height:220px;" target="_blank" title="邂逅泉八戒忘形">
<img alt="邂逅泉八戒忘形" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss0.bdstatic.com/-4o3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=d6299c3263d0f703e2b292de38fa5148/37d3d539b6003af366bd1645342ac65c1038b694.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:182px;height:220px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
邂逅泉八戒忘形
</span>
</div>这一点猪八戒尤其出色。不论是在天上做天蓬元帅时调戏霓裳仙子；还是做了妖怪之后，先取卯二姐为妻，后硬做<a href="/item/%E9%AB%98%E8%80%81%E5%BA%84" target="_blank">高老庄</a>的女婿；以及取经路上看见美女就流口水走不动路，都可以充分说明。在<a href="/item/%E5%A5%B3%E5%84%BF%E5%9B%BD" target="_blank">女儿国</a>时那个美丽的女王，就曾经让老猪动心不已，在蜘蛛精在洗澡时，变黑鱼去调戏。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><b>胆小</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">对于我们这样一个泱泱大国而言，而且是正处于默默发展经济的非常时期，选择什么样的人十分重要。做人稳重，处事谨慎，是组织人事部门优先考虑的因素。说白了就是选胆小的人唐僧师徒四人：师傅迂腐、师兄高傲、师弟<a href="/item/%E8%85%B9%E9%BB%91" target="_blank">腹黑</a>，唯有猪八戒一人胆小。西行路上，各路妖魔鬼怪大都是神通广大之流。所以猪八戒就常常害怕一不小心自己被那些无法无天的东西给吃了。长时间的担惊受怕，造就了猪八戒胆小怕事的性格。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="6"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_6"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="影视形象"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-2" label-module="para-title">
<h2 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>影视形象</h2>
<a class="edit-icon j-edit-link" data-edit-dl="6" href="javascript:;"><em class="cmn-icon wiki-lemma-icons wiki-lemma-icons_edit-lemma"></em>编辑</a>
</div>
<div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="6_1"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_6_1"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="彭鹏"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="6-1"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>彭鹏</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">Peng Peng，<a href="/item/%E9%A6%99%E6%B8%AF%E9%82%B5%E6%B0%8F%E7%94%B5%E5%BD%B1" target="_blank">香港邵氏电影</a>男演员，活跃于1959 -1976 年<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:220px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/b90e7bec54e736d1a1a3490298504fc2d562690c?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:220px;height:214px;" target="_blank" title="">
<img alt="" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss2.bdstatic.com/-fo3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=59a79063262dd42a5b0906a9333a5b2f/b90e7bec54e736d1a1a3490298504fc2d562690c.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:220px;height:214px;"/>
</a>
</div>。彭鹏原名<a href="/item/%E7%8E%8B%E5%BF%97%E5%B9%B3" target="_blank">王志平</a>，出生于广东，1959 年来港，加盟邵氏，多出演喜剧角色。其中以在《<a href="/item/%E8%A5%BF%E6%B8%B8%E8%AE%B0" target="_blank">西游记</a>》系列中扮演的猪八戒最受欢迎。最后一部邵氏作品是《<i><a href="/item/%E5%A4%A7%E8%80%81%E5%8D%83" target="_blank">大老千</a></i>》（1975），现已息影多年。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><b><br/>　　</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><b><br/>　　</b></div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="6_2"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_6_2"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="马德华"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="6-2"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>马德华</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><a data-lemmaid="11925" href="/item/%E9%A9%AC%E5%BE%B7%E5%8D%8E/11925" target="_blank">马德华</a>，1945 年 8 月 11 日生于北京，祖籍山东省武城县，回族<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:173px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/50da81cb39dbb6fd02de582c0a24ab18972b3736?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:173px;height:220px;" target="_blank" title="马德华版猪八戒">
<img alt="马德华版猪八戒" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss0.bdstatic.com/94o3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=9c07e4bb830a19d8cf03830703fb82c9/50da81cb39dbb6fd02de582c0a24ab18972b3736.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:173px;height:220px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
马德华版猪八戒
</span>
</div>，北方<a href="/item/%E6%98%86%E5%89%A7" target="_blank">昆剧</a>院演员，<a href="/item/%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E4%B8%80%E7%BA%A7%E6%BC%94%E5%91%98" target="_blank">国家一级演员</a>。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">1985 年首次出演与<a href="/item/%E5%85%AD%E5%B0%8F%E9%BE%84%E7%AB%A5" target="_blank">六小龄童</a>、<a href="/item/%E6%B1%AA%E7%B2%A4" target="_blank">汪粤</a>、<a data-lemmaid="6496" href="/item/%E5%BE%90%E5%B0%91%E5%8D%8E/6496" target="_blank">徐少华</a>、<a href="/item/%E8%BF%9F%E9%87%8D%E7%91%9E" target="_blank">迟重瑞</a>主演的古装神话剧《<a href="/item/%E8%A5%BF%E6%B8%B8%E8%AE%B0" target="_blank">西游记</a>》饰演猪八戒。2006 年在<a href="/item/%E5%BC%A0%E7%82%AC" target="_blank">张炬</a>、<a href="/item/%E8%B0%A2%E8%8A%B3" target="_blank">谢芳</a>主演的电视剧《<a href="/item/%E8%80%81%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%95%85%E4%BA%8B" target="_blank">老人的故事</a>》中饰演施老头。同年主演喜剧片《瞧，这一担挑儿》。2007 年与六小龄童、<a href="/item/%E5%88%98%E5%A4%A7%E5%88%9A" target="_blank">刘大刚</a>、迟重瑞领衔主演大型神话 3D 立体电视剧《<a href="/item/%E5%90%B4%E6%89%BF%E6%81%A9%E4%B8%8E%E8%A5%BF%E6%B8%B8%E8%AE%B0" target="_blank">吴承恩与西游记</a>》再次饰演猪八戒。2011 年在<a href="/item/%E5%BA%B7%E5%AE%81" target="_blank">康宁</a>指导的电视剧《<a href="/item/%E5%86%92%E7%89%8C%E8%91%A3%E4%BA%8B%E9%95%BF" target="_blank">冒牌董事长</a>》中饰演廖总。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="6_3"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_6_3"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="崔景富"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="6-3"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>崔景富</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><a href="/item/%E5%B4%94%E6%99%AF%E5%AF%8C" target="_blank">崔景富</a>（Cui Jingfu），汉族，1951 年4 月生于辽宁省北票县。<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:149px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/9c16fdfaaf51f3de0ca85a6e97eef01f3a2979a6?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:149px;height:220px;" target="_blank" title="崔景富版猪八戒">
<img alt="崔景富版猪八戒" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss0.bdstatic.com/94o3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=8d0d10661338534388cf8023a313b01f/9c16fdfaaf51f3de0ca85a6e97eef01f3a2979a6.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:149px;height:220px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
崔景富版猪八戒
</span>
</div>幼时家境贫寒。在五间房初中读书时即热衷于表演艺术。1970 年在北漂进入专业表演艺术团体，即而成为深受观众喜爱的主要演员。崔景富毕业于<a href="/item/%E4%B8%AD%E5%A4%AE%E6%88%8F%E5%89%A7%E5%AD%A6%E9%99%A2" target="_blank">中央戏剧学院</a>86届表演系干部专修班。现任职<a href="/item/%E5%B9%BF%E5%B7%9E%E8%AF%9D%E5%89%A7%E5%9B%A2" target="_blank">广州话剧团</a>，系著名的主要演员，曾多次获国家级大奖和省级大奖，并立国家文化系统三等功。<a href="/item/%E4%B8%AD%E5%9B%BD%E6%88%8F%E5%89%A7%E5%AE%B6%E5%8D%8F%E4%BC%9A" target="_blank">中国戏剧家协会</a>会员、<a href="/item/%E4%B8%AD%E5%9B%BD%E7%94%B5%E8%A7%86%E8%89%BA%E6%9C%AF%E5%AE%B6%E5%8D%8F%E4%BC%9A" target="_blank">中国电视艺术家协会</a>会员。被编入《当代中国电视人》、《中国戏剧家大辞典》等典籍。崔景富是<a href="/item/%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E4%B8%80%E7%BA%A7%E6%BC%94%E5%91%98" target="_blank">国家一级演员</a>，全国著名话剧表演艺术家，最熟悉的是《西游记续集》中的猪八戒。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="6_4"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_6_4"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="臧金生"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="6-4"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>臧金生</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">2012 担演张纪中版《西游记》猪八戒。<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:220px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/8d5494eef01f3a29903f36c49a25bc315d607cc1?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:220px;height:156px;" target="_blank" title="臧金生版猪八戒">
<img alt="臧金生版猪八戒" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss1.bdstatic.com/-vo3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=0fdb4529b37eca8016053ee5a1229712/8d5494eef01f3a29903f36c49a25bc315d607cc1.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:220px;height:156px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
臧金生版猪八戒
</span>
</div></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><a href="/item/%E8%87%A7%E9%87%91%E7%94%9F" target="_blank">臧金生</a>，1959 年生于天津。著名演员。1986 年毕业于<a href="/item/%E5%8C%97%E4%BA%AC%E7%94%B5%E5%BD%B1%E5%AD%A6%E9%99%A2" target="_blank">北京电影学院</a>表演系，入<a href="/item/%E5%8C%97%E4%BA%AC%E7%94%B5%E5%BD%B1%E5%88%B6%E7%89%87%E5%8E%82" target="_blank">北京电影制片厂</a>。2003 年毕业于<a href="/item/%E5%8C%97%E4%BA%AC%E5%A4%A7%E5%AD%A6" target="_blank">北京大学</a>艺术学系。<a href="/item/%E4%B8%AD%E5%9B%BD%E7%94%B5%E5%BD%B1%E9%9B%86%E5%9B%A2%E5%85%AC%E5%8F%B8" target="_blank">中国电影集团公司</a>艺术创作中心业务发展部主任，<a href="/item/%E4%B8%AD%E5%9B%BD%E7%94%B5%E5%BD%B1%E5%AE%B6%E5%8D%8F%E4%BC%9A" target="_blank">中国电影家协会</a>会员，中国电视艺术家协会会员，中国广播电视学会会员，中国电影基金会艺术委员会委员。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="6_5"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_6_5"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="黎耀祥"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="6-5"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>黎耀祥</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">在 TVB 版《西游记》中饰演猪八戒，合作者张卫健、<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:220px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/472309f790529822d81e8794deca7bcb0a46d4bc?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:220px;height:165px;" target="_blank" title="">
<img alt="" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss2.bdstatic.com/9fo3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=2c08bd1dd3b44aed5d4eb9e6831c876a/472309f790529822d81e8794deca7bcb0a46d4bc.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:220px;height:165px;"/>
</a>
</div>陈浩民。最聪明、最贱的猪八戒。经典语句：多情自古空余恨，此恨绵绵无绝期</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><a href="/item/%E9%BB%8E%E8%80%80%E7%A5%A5" target="_blank">黎耀祥</a>，1983 年加入<a data-lemmaid="16404496" href="/item/%E6%97%A0%E7%BA%BF%E7%94%B5%E8%A7%86/16404496" target="_blank">无线电视</a>成为营业部文员，后进入无线艺员训练班学习。1986 年开始参演电视剧。1998～2002 年，到亚洲电视和影坛发展，2002 年重返无线电视，在《<a href="/item/%E7%A7%80%E6%89%8D%E9%81%87%E7%9D%80%E5%85%B5" target="_blank">秀才遇着兵</a>》、《<a href="/item/%E6%A5%9A%E6%B1%89%E9%AA%84%E9%9B%84" target="_blank">楚汉骄雄</a>》等剧集担演男配角。2009 年开始担纲剧集第一男主角，同年凭借《<a href="/item/%E5%B7%BE%E5%B8%BC%E6%9E%AD%E9%9B%84" target="_blank">巾帼枭雄</a>》夺得<a href="/item/%E4%B8%87%E5%8D%83%E6%98%9F%E8%BE%89%E9%A2%81%E5%A5%96%E5%85%B8%E7%A4%BC" target="_blank">万千星辉颁奖典礼</a>“最佳男主角”。2010 年在第 44 届万千星辉颁奖典礼中，祥仔凭借《<a href="/item/%E5%B7%BE%E5%B8%BC%E6%9E%AD%E9%9B%84%E4%B9%8B%E4%B9%89%E6%B5%B7%E8%B1%AA%E6%83%85" target="_blank">巾帼枭雄之义海豪情</a>》蝉联“最佳男主角”奖项。2012 年黎耀祥凭《<a href="/item/%E5%A4%A7%E5%A4%AA%E7%9B%91" target="_blank">大太监</a>》中<a data-lemmaid="17427" href="/item/%E6%9D%8E%E8%8E%B2%E8%8B%B1/17427" target="_blank">李莲英</a>一角，三度问鼎“最佳男主角”。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="6_6"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_6_6"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="谢宁"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="6-6"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>谢宁</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><a data-lemmaid="10987557" href="/item/%E8%B0%A2%E5%AE%81/10987557" target="_blank">谢宁</a>，浙江版《西游记》中饰演猪八戒，同样也在《<a href="/item/%E5%AE%9D%E8%8E%B2%E7%81%AF" target="_blank">宝莲灯</a>》<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:146px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/91529822720e0cf3b552a0f10946f21fbe09aa17?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:146px;height:220px;" target="_blank" title="谢宁版猪八戒">
<img alt="谢宁版猪八戒" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss2.bdstatic.com/9fo3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=b82c91d72d738bd4c021b533918a876c/91529822720e0cf3b552a0f10946f21fbe09aa17.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:146px;height:220px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
谢宁版猪八戒
</span>
</div>、《<a href="/item/%E9%AD%94%E5%B9%BB%E6%89%8B" target="_blank">魔幻手</a><a href="/item/%E6%9C%BA" target="_blank">机</a>》系列中饰演猪八戒。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">1964 年 10 年 09 日出生于中国北京，毕业于 96 届师大艺术系。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">1994 年，参演<a href="/item/%E9%BB%84%E6%B3%B0%E6%9D%A5" target="_blank">黄泰来</a>执导，<a href="/item/%E5%88%98%E5%BE%B7%E5%8D%8E" target="_blank">刘德华</a>、<a href="/item/%E6%9E%97%E9%9D%92%E9%9C%9E" target="_blank">林青霞</a>、<a data-lemmaid="43325" href="/item/%E5%BE%90%E9%94%A6%E6%B1%9F/43325" target="_blank">徐锦江</a>共同主演的古装武侠剧《<a href="/item/%E5%88%80%E5%89%91%E7%AC%91" target="_blank">刀剑笑</a>》。2001 年，在<a href="/item/%E9%83%91%E5%85%8B%E6%B4%AA" target="_blank">郑克洪</a>执导的古装历史剧《<a href="/item/%E6%AD%A6%E5%9C%A3%E5%85%B3%E5%85%AC" target="_blank">武圣关公</a>》中饰许禇。2004年 6 月，拍摄中央台投资的神话剧《<a href="/item/%E7%99%BD%E8%9B%87%E4%BC%A0" target="_blank">白蛇传</a>》。2005 年，搭档<a href="/item/%E6%9B%B9%E9%AA%8F" target="_blank">曹骏</a>、<a data-lemmaid="143783" href="/item/%E8%88%92%E7%95%85/143783" target="_blank">舒畅</a>、<a href="/item/%E7%84%A6%E6%81%A9%E4%BF%8A" target="_blank">焦恩俊</a>主演神话剧《<a href="/item/%E5%AE%9D%E8%8E%B2%E7%81%AF" target="_blank">宝莲灯</a>》。2006 年，与<a data-lemmaid="24135" href="/item/%E6%9D%8E%E6%BB%A8/24135" target="_blank">李滨</a>、舒畅、焦恩俊共同主演现代神话科幻喜剧《<a href="/item/%E9%AD%94%E5%B9%BB%E6%89%8B%E6%9C%BA" target="_blank">魔幻手机</a>》。2007 年 8 月，拍摄<a href="/item/%E4%BD%99%E6%98%8E%E7%94%9F" target="_blank">余明生</a>执导的古装神话剧《<a href="/item/%E5%AE%9D%E8%8E%B2%E7%81%AF%E5%89%8D%E4%BC%A0" target="_blank">宝莲灯前传</a>》。2009 年，搭档<a href="/item/%E8%B4%B9%E6%8C%AF%E7%BF%94" target="_blank">费振翔</a>、<a href="/item/%E9%99%88%E5%8F%B8%E7%BF%B0" target="_blank">陈司翰</a>、<a href="/item/%E7%89%9F%E5%87%A4%E5%BD%AC" target="_blank">牟凤彬</a>参与<a href="/item/%E7%A8%8B%E5%8A%9B%E6%A0%8B" target="_blank">程力栋</a>执导的浙江新版《<a href="/item/%E8%A5%BF%E6%B8%B8%E8%AE%B0" target="_blank">西游记</a>》。2011 年，与李滨、舒畅、<a data-lemmaid="33767" href="/item/%E5%88%98%E7%BE%8E%E5%B8%8C/33767" target="_blank">刘美希</a>共同主演现代魔幻剧《魔幻手机 2 傻妞归来》。2013 年，搭档<a data-lemmaid="76206" href="/item/%E5%88%98%E5%A9%89%E5%A9%B7/76206" target="_blank">刘婉婷</a>、<a data-lemmaid="2357597" href="/item/%E5%BC%A0%E6%B5%A9%E7%84%B6/2357597" target="_blank">张浩然</a>领衔主演独特形式儿童系列剧《<a href="/item/%E5%A5%87%E5%A6%99%E5%B0%8F%E9%95%87" target="_blank">奇妙小镇</a>》。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="6_7"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_6_7"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="伊藤淳史"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="6-7"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>伊藤淳史</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">在 2006 版的日本版西游记饰演猪八戒。<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:220px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/55e736d12f2eb9380532adf8d6628535e5dd6f59?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:220px;height:119px;" target="_blank" title="伊藤淳史版猪八戒">
<img alt="伊藤淳史版猪八戒" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss2.bdstatic.com/-fo3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=bb4f36102b34349b70066987f9eb1521/55e736d12f2eb9380532adf8d6628535e5dd6f59.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:220px;height:119px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
伊藤淳史版猪八戒
</span>
</div></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><a href="/item/%E4%BC%8A%E8%97%A4%E6%B7%B3%E5%8F%B2" target="_blank">伊藤淳史</a>（1983 年 11 月 25 日－）是日本千叶县船桥市出身的演员，就读法政大学经营学部毕业。所属于四分音经纪公司（クォータートーン）。弟弟<a href="/item/%E4%BC%8A%E8%97%A4%E9%9A%86%E5%A4%A7" target="_blank">伊藤隆大</a>（已故）也同样是演员。童星出身，在“爆笑假面战士”里饰演迷你假面战士而开始活跃，后来在“卡路里伙伴”的广告里以“年轻人加油！”的台词而出名。因《<a data-lemmaid="1347978" href="/item/%E7%94%B5%E8%BD%A6%E7%94%B7/1347978" target="_blank">电车男</a>》一剧而在香港、澳门、台湾广为人知。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><b>日本版猪八戒</b>（右边这只猪（虽然不太分不清谁是猪八戒但日本货但到这种水平已经很不错了））。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="6_8"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_6_8"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="吴孟达"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="6-8"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>吴孟达</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">在《<a data-lemmaid="9640" href="/item/%E5%A4%A7%E8%AF%9D%E8%A5%BF%E6%B8%B8/9640" target="_blank">大话西游</a>》中饰演猪八戒。<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:220px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/1c950a7b02087bf4342580e3f1d3572c10dfcfeb?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:220px;height:123px;" target="_blank" title="吴孟达版猪八戒">
<img alt="吴孟达版猪八戒" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss2.bdstatic.com/-fo3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=9afba9c1f8edab6470724ac2c737af81/1c950a7b02087bf4342580e3f1d3572c10dfcfeb.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:220px;height:123px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
吴孟达版猪八戒
</span>
</div></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><a data-lemmaid="18269" href="/item/%E5%90%B4%E5%AD%9F%E8%BE%BE/18269" target="_blank">吴孟达</a>，香港男演员，1953 年 1 月 2 日出生于福建厦门，七岁随父母移居至<a data-lemmaid="128775" href="/item/%E9%A6%99%E6%B8%AF/128775" target="_blank">香港</a>。在香港电影中与<a href="/item/%E5%91%A8%E6%98%9F%E9%A9%B0" target="_blank">周星驰</a>合作成为搞笑<a href="/item/%E6%97%A0%E5%8E%98%E5%A4%B4" target="_blank">无厘头</a>的黄金搭档。吴孟达被电影界尊称为“达哥”，是金牌配角，被誉为香港和华语影坛片酬最高的黄金配角，也曾获得多届<a href="/item/%E9%A6%99%E6%B8%AF%E7%94%B5%E5%BD%B1%E9%87%91%E5%83%8F%E5%A5%96" target="_blank">香港电影金像奖</a>和<a href="/item/%E5%8F%B0%E6%B9%BE%E7%94%B5%E5%BD%B1%E9%87%91%E9%A9%AC%E5%A5%96" target="_blank">台湾电影金马奖</a>最佳男配角提名，并荣获第十届香港电影金像奖最佳男配角。其御用配音演员是<a href="/item/%E8%83%A1%E7%AB%8B%E6%88%90" target="_blank">胡立成</a>。1973 年投考了无线电视的艺员培训班；最重要的配角演员之一。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="6_9"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_6_9"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="徐峥"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="6-9"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>徐峥</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">在《<a data-lemmaid="29506" href="/item/%E6%98%A5%E5%85%89%E7%81%BF%E7%83%82%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/29506" target="_blank">春光灿烂猪八戒</a>》中饰演猪八戒。<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:138px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/8435e5dde71190ef3d8591e1c71b9d16fdfa6095?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:138px;height:220px;" target="_blank" title="">
<img alt="" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss3.bdstatic.com/-Po3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=5e8d00dddc39b60049ce08b5d9503526/8435e5dde71190ef3d8591e1c71b9d16fdfa6095.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:138px;height:220px;"/>
</a>
</div></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">徐峥，1972 年 4 月 18 日出生于上海，中国内地男演员、导演。1994 年毕业于<a href="/item/%E4%B8%8A%E6%B5%B7%E6%88%8F%E5%89%A7%E5%AD%A6%E9%99%A2" target="_blank">上海戏剧学院</a>。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">1998 年出演话剧《股票的颜色》获得第十届<a href="/item/%E7%99%BD%E7%8E%89%E5%85%B0%E6%88%8F%E5%89%A7%E5%A5%96" target="_blank">白玉兰戏剧奖</a>最佳男主角奖。2000 年参演《春光灿烂猪八戒》饰演猪八戒走红；2002 年参演《<a href="/item/%E6%9D%8E%E5%8D%AB%E5%BD%93%E5%AE%98" target="_blank">李卫当官</a>》饰演李卫。2006 年在电影《<a href="/item/%E7%96%AF%E7%8B%82%E7%9A%84%E7%9F%B3%E5%A4%B4" target="_blank">疯狂的石头</a>》客串反派冯董。2007 年主演贺岁喜剧电影《<a href="/item/%E7%88%B1%E6%83%85%E5%91%BC%E5%8F%AB%E8%BD%AC%E7%A7%BB" target="_blank">爱情呼叫转移</a>》。2010 年主演电影《<a href="/item/%E4%BA%BA%E5%9C%A8%E5%9B%A7%E9%80%94" target="_blank">人在囧途</a>》饰演老板。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">2012 年，自编、自导、自演的喜剧电影《<a href="/item/%E4%BA%BA%E5%86%8D%E5%9B%A7%E9%80%94%E4%B9%8B%E6%B3%B0%E5%9B%A7" target="_blank">人再囧途之泰囧</a>》上映 5 天票房突破 3 亿，创造华语片首周票房纪录，上映一个月票房达到 12 亿，最终票房 12.69 亿，成为中国电影市场华语片票房冠军。2013 年，在电影《<a href="/item/%E6%91%A9%E7%99%BB%E5%B9%B4%E4%BB%A3" target="_blank">摩登年代</a>》中首次出任监制。2014 年，主演的电影《<a href="/item/%E6%97%A0%E4%BA%BA%E5%8C%BA" target="_blank">无人区</a>》入围第 64 届<a href="/item/%E6%9F%8F%E6%9E%97%E5%9B%BD%E9%99%85%E7%94%B5%E5%BD%B1%E8%8A%82" target="_blank">柏林国际电影节</a>主竞赛单元影片。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="6_10"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_6_10"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="黄海波"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="6-10"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>黄海波</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">在《<a href="/item/%E7%A6%8F%E6%98%9F%E9%AB%98%E7%85%A7%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92" target="_blank">福星高照猪八戒</a>》中饰演猪八戒。<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:165px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/d8f9d72a6059252dbed2cc0e379b033b5ab5b9f7?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:165px;height:220px;" target="_blank" title="黄海波版猪八戒">
<img alt="黄海波版猪八戒" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss2.bdstatic.com/9fo3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=04fef9af097b020808c938e352d8f25f/d8f9d72a6059252dbed2cc0e379b033b5ab5b9f7.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:165px;height:220px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
黄海波版猪八戒
</span>
</div></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">1976 年 11 月 25 日生于天津市蓟县，中国大陆男演员，2001 年毕业于<a href="/item/%E5%8C%97%E4%BA%AC%E7%94%B5%E5%BD%B1%E5%AD%A6%E9%99%A2" target="_blank">北京电影学院</a>表演系本科班。2001 年参演<a href="/item/%E5%BA%B7%E6%B4%AA%E9%9B%B7" target="_blank">康洪雷</a>导演的《<a data-lemmaid="4507532" href="/item/%E6%BF%80%E6%83%85%E7%87%83%E7%83%A7%E7%9A%84%E5%B2%81%E6%9C%88/4507532" target="_blank">激情燃烧的岁月</a>》，开始走上了演艺道路。 2007 年，参演由<a href="/item/%E9%AB%98%E5%B8%8C%E5%B8%8C" target="_blank">高希希</a>导演的《<a data-lemmaid="11006780" href="/item/%E6%96%B0%E4%B8%8A%E6%B5%B7%E6%BB%A9/11006780" target="_blank">新上海滩</a>》 ，2010 年在与<a href="/item/%E6%B5%B7%E6%B8%85" target="_blank">海清</a>合作的电视剧《<a data-lemmaid="14734" href="/item/%E5%AA%B3%E5%A6%87%E7%9A%84%E7%BE%8E%E5%A5%BD%E6%97%B6%E4%BB%A3/14734" target="_blank">媳妇的美好时代</a>》中饰演“余味”一角，该剧获得第 28 届<a href="/item/%E9%A3%9E%E5%A4%A9%E5%A5%96" target="_blank">飞天奖</a>、第 25 届<a href="/item/%E9%87%91%E9%B9%B0%E5%A5%96" target="_blank">金鹰奖</a>优秀电视剧奖。 2012 年因主演的抗日战争故事《<a href="/item/%E6%B0%B8%E4%B8%8D%E7%A3%A8%E7%81%AD%E7%9A%84%E7%95%AA%E5%8F%B7" target="_blank">永不磨灭的番号</a>》获得第 18 届<a href="/item/%E4%B8%8A%E6%B5%B7%E7%94%B5%E8%A7%86%E8%8A%82%E7%99%BD%E7%8E%89%E5%85%B0%E5%A5%96" target="_blank">上海电视节白玉兰奖</a>最佳男演员奖。2013 年，主演央视和湖南卫视合拍的热播剧《<a data-lemmaid="66672" href="/item/%E5%92%B1%E4%BB%AC%E7%BB%93%E5%A9%9A%E5%90%A7/66672" target="_blank">咱们结婚吧</a>》。 2014 年 6 月，主演电影《胜利》获得第 17 届上海国际电影节评委会大奖。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><b>黄海波版猪八戒</b>。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="6_11"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_6_11"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="古巨基"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="6-11"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>古巨基</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><a href="/item/%E5%8F%A4%E5%B7%A8%E5%9F%BA" target="_blank">古巨基</a>，1972年8月18日出生于香港，歌手、演员、主持<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:220px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/d788d43f8794a4c29a1435210df41bd5ad6e3981?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:220px;height:146px;" target="_blank" title="古巨基版猪八戒">
<img alt="古巨基版猪八戒" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss3.bdstatic.com/7Po3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=2c19ae6e0a23dd542573a06ae109b3df/d788d43f8794a4c29a1435210df41bd5ad6e3981.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:220px;height:146px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
古巨基版猪八戒
</span>
</div>人，毕业于沙田官立中学。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">1991 年考入<a href="/item/%E6%97%A0%E7%BA%BF%E7%94%B5%E8%A7%86%E8%89%BA%E5%91%98%E8%AE%AD%E7%BB%83%E7%8F%AD" target="_blank">无线电视艺员训练班</a>，早年担任主持人。1994 年推出首张专辑《<a href="/item/%E7%88%B1%E7%9A%84%E8%A7%A3%E9%87%8A" target="_blank">爱的解释</a>》正式进军乐坛，同年获得香港乐坛四台音乐颁奖典礼的男新人金奖。2001 年出演电视剧《<a href="/item/%E6%83%85%E6%B7%B1%E6%B7%B1%E9%9B%A8%E8%92%99%E8%92%99" target="_blank">情深深雨蒙蒙</a>》，饰演<a href="/item/%E4%BD%95%E4%B9%A6%E6%A1%93" target="_blank">何书桓</a>一角。2003 年重返香港乐坛。2008 年<a href="/item/%E5%A4%8F%E5%AD%A3%E5%A5%A5%E6%9E%97%E5%8C%B9%E5%85%8B%E8%BF%90%E5%8A%A8%E4%BC%9A" target="_blank">夏季奥林匹克运动会</a>担任香港区火炬接力第八棒火炬手。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">《<a href="/item/%E6%98%A5%E5%85%89%E7%81%BF%E7%83%82%E4%B9%8B%E6%AC%A2%E4%B9%90%E5%85%83%E5%B8%85" target="_blank">春光灿烂之欢乐元帅</a>》是由福纳影视公司巨资投拍的全新神话喜剧。讲述古巨基扮演的男主角从猪到人再到元帅的历程，共分为两部：《欢乐元帅 1》（八大戒、天崩地裂爱死你）与《欢乐元帅 2 》（三戏孙悟空、惊天动地抢新娘）。2011 年 4 月 28 日，本剧在昆山福纳影视基地举行了开机仪式，已于 2012 年 1 月在各大卫视上映。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="6_12"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_6_12"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="陈炳强"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="6-12"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>陈炳强</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><a href="/item/%E9%99%88%E7%82%B3%E5%BC%BA" target="_blank">陈炳强</a>，1990 年 7 月 27 日出生于广东省揭阳市惠来县<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:220px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/c8ea15ce36d3d539c657ddc93987e950352ab056?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:220px;height:140px;" target="_blank" title="陈炳强版猪八戒">
<img alt="陈炳强版猪八戒" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss0.bdstatic.com/94o3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=61884ed68913632711edc531a18ea056/c8ea15ce36d3d539c657ddc93987e950352ab056.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:220px;height:140px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
陈炳强版猪八戒
</span>
</div>，毕业于惠来县华侨中学。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">2011 年陈炳强参演曾周星驰导演的电影《<a href="/item/%E8%A5%BF%E6%B8%B8%C2%B7%E9%99%8D%E9%AD%94%E7%AF%87" target="_blank">西游·降魔篇</a>》中饰演猪刚鬣一角而受到关注；同年客串古装剧《<a href="/item/%E5%80%BE%E4%B8%96%E7%9A%87%E5%A6%83" target="_blank">倾世皇妃</a>》；2012 年客串《<a href="/item/%E7%9A%87%E7%B2%AE%E8%83%A1%E5%90%8C%E5%8D%81%E4%B9%9D%E5%8F%B7" target="_blank">皇粮胡同十九号</a>》；2013 年出演网络剧《<a href="/item/%E4%BA%BA%E7%94%9F%E9%9C%80%E8%A6%81%E6%8F%AD%E7%A9%BF" target="_blank">人生需要揭穿</a>》并客串《<a href="/item/%E9%99%86%E8%B4%9E%E4%BC%A0%E5%A5%87" target="_blank">陆贞传奇</a>》。2015年10月16日其主演的电影《<a href="/item/%E7%AC%94%E4%BB%99%E9%AD%94%E5%92%92" target="_blank">笔仙魔咒</a>》正式上映 。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="6_13"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_6_13"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="高鑫"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="6-13"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>高鑫</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">高鑫，在 2004 年的《<a href="/item/%E5%96%9C%E6%B0%94%E6%B4%8B%E6%B4%8B%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92" target="_blank">喜气洋洋猪八戒</a>》中饰演猪八戒。19<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:220px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/2e2eb9389b504fc24eea620fe6dde71190ef6d07?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:220px;height:178px;" target="_blank" title="高鑫版猪八戒">
<img alt="高鑫版猪八戒" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss3.bdstatic.com/-Po3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=b3bcd3a1003b5bb5bad727fc06d2d523/2e2eb9389b504fc24eea620fe6dde71190ef6d07.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:220px;height:178px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
高鑫版猪八戒
</span>
</div>76 年 12 月 11 日生于北京市，中国内地男演员，毕业于<a href="/item/%E5%8C%97%E4%BA%AC%E7%94%B5%E5%BD%B1%E5%AD%A6%E9%99%A2" target="_blank">北京电影学院</a>表演系。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">2001 年，凭借电视剧《<a href="/item/%E6%83%85%E6%B7%B1%E6%B7%B1%E9%9B%A8%E6%BF%9B%E6%BF%9B" target="_blank">情深深雨濛濛</a>》中陆尔豪一角而获得台湾<a href="/item/%E9%87%91%E9%92%9F%E5%A5%96" target="_blank">金钟奖</a>最佳新人奖。2003 年，在电视剧《喜气洋洋猪八戒》中饰演猪八戒而被观众所熟知。2005 年，在电视剧《<a href="/item/%E6%96%B0%E9%86%89%E6%89%93%E9%87%91%E6%9E%9D" target="_blank">新醉打金枝</a>》中饰演李权。2013 年在电视剧《<a href="/item/%E5%88%B0%E7%88%B1%E7%9A%84%E8%B7%9D%E7%A6%BB" target="_blank">到爱的距离</a>》中韦天舒饰演。2014 年，在电视剧《<a href="/item/%E7%90%85%E7%90%8A%E6%A6%9C" target="_blank">琅琊榜</a>》中饰演太子。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="6_14"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_6_14"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="周德华"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="6-14"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>周德华</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><a data-lemmaid="5863271" href="/item/%E5%91%A8%E5%BE%B7%E5%8D%8E/5863271" target="_blank">周德华</a>，在 2005 版的《<a data-lemmaid="6860314" href="/item/%E7%BA%A2%E5%AD%A9%E5%84%BF/6860314" target="_blank">红孩儿</a>》中饰演猪八戒。<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:220px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/8718367adab44aed2b848d35b71c8701a08bfb1c?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:220px;height:146px;" target="_blank" title="周德华版猪八戒">
<img alt="周德华版猪八戒" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss1.bdstatic.com/-vo3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=d5e10fc5af18972ba73a07c8d6cf7b9d/8718367adab44aed2b848d35b71c8701a08bfb1c.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:220px;height:146px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
周德华版猪八戒
</span>
</div></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">周德华，男，1980 年 9 月生，大陆演员。曾出演《<a href="/item/%E5%A4%A9%E7%9C%9F%E9%81%87%E5%88%B0%E7%8E%B0%E5%AE%9E" target="_blank">天真遇到现实</a>》、《<a href="/item/%E4%BC%BC%E6%B0%B4%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8E" target="_blank">似水年华</a>》、《<a href="/item/%E7%BE%8E%E4%B8%BD%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%8B" target="_blank">美丽的事</a>》、《<a href="/item/%E5%A4%A9%E5%A4%96%E9%A3%9E%E4%BB%99" target="_blank">天外飞仙</a>》、《<a data-lemmaid="2943573" href="/item/%E5%94%B1%E6%88%98%E8%AE%B0/2943573" target="_blank">唱战记</a>》等电视剧。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="7"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_7"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="影视相关"></a>

</div></div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="7_1"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_7_1"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="影视作品"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="7-1"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>影视作品</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒（虚幻人物）是个被人们喜爱同情的喜剧人物，特别是<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:220px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/b17eca8065380cd7f90497cba044ad34598281f9?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:220px;height:165px;" target="_blank" title="彭鹏饰演的猪八戒">
<img alt="彭鹏饰演的猪八戒" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://gss0.bdstatic.com/94o3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=2b316d344e4a20a4351e3bc5a0529847/b17eca8065380cd7f90497cba044ad34598281f9.jpg" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" style="width:220px;height:165px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
彭鹏饰演的猪八戒
</span>
</div>现代，越来越被人喜欢了，仅以猪八戒为主题的电视剧就拍下好几部，如《魔幻手机》、《春光灿烂猪八戒》、《福星高照猪八戒》、《喜气洋洋猪八戒》、《浙版新西游记》等等。妙趣横生，语言幽默，画面精美，无一不逗人乐，招人爱，还有动画片《天上掉下个猪八戒》、《<a href="/item/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92%E5%90%83%E8%A5%BF%E7%93%9C" target="_blank">猪八戒吃西瓜</a>》。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">电视剧《<a data-lemmaid="4919803" href="/item/%E5%AE%9D%E8%8E%B2%E7%81%AF/4919803" target="_blank">宝莲灯</a>》中，猪八戒还为沉香、丁香、敖春担任师傅，观众将他戏弄为“最滑稽的师傅”。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="7_2"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_7_2"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="音乐"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="7-2"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>音乐</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">电影《西游降魔》歌曲。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">出现了一些以猪八戒为对象而创作的歌曲，比如，<a href="/item/%E6%9B%B9%E5%B0%94%E7%9C%9F" target="_blank">曹尔真</a>演唱的《<a href="/item/%E6%88%91%E6%98%AF%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92" target="_blank">我是猪八戒</a>》，还有如《<a href="/item/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92%E4%B9%8B%E6%AD%8C" target="_blank">猪八戒之歌</a>》、《<a href="/item/%E5%A5%BD%E6%98%A5%E5%85%89" target="_blank">好春光</a>》、《<a href="/item/%E6%88%91%E7%88%B1%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92" target="_blank">我爱猪八戒</a>》、《猪八戒》、《话说猪八戒》、《<a href="/item/%E5%BF%AB%E4%B9%90%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92" target="_blank">快乐猪八戒</a>》、《<a href="/item/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92%E8%83%8C%E5%AA%B3%E5%A6%87" target="_blank">猪八戒背媳妇</a>》、《要爱就爱猪八戒》等等。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">《<b>猪八戒之歌</b>》</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">词：<a href="/item/%E9%98%8E%E8%82%83" target="_blank">阎肃</a></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">曲：<a href="/item/%E8%AE%B8%E9%95%9C%E6%B8%85" target="_blank">许镜清</a></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">唱：<a href="/item/%E9%A9%AC%E5%9B%BD%E5%85%89" target="_blank">马国光</a></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><b>　</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><b>歌曲：</b>《<b><a href="/item/%E5%A5%BD%E6%98%A5%E5%85%89" target="_blank">好春光</a></b>》</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">演唱者：吴桐</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><b>歌曲：</b>《<b><a href="/item/%E6%88%91%E7%88%B1%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92" target="_blank">我爱猪八戒</a></b>》</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">演唱者：张拉拉</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a class="lemma-anchor para-title" name="8"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="sub5039852_8"></a>
<a class="lemma-anchor " name="歇后语"></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-2" label-module="para-title">
<h2 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">猪八戒</span>歇后语</h2>
<a class="edit-icon j-edit-link" data-edit-dl="8" href="javascript:;"><em class="cmn-icon wiki-lemma-icons wiki-lemma-icons_edit-lemma"></em>编辑</a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒照镜子—<b>里外不是人</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒败阵—<a href="/item/%E5%80%92%E6%89%93%E4%B8%80%E8%80%99" target="_blank"><b>倒打一耙</b></a></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒看唱本—<b>冒充识字人</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒戴花—<b>越多越丑</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒做梦娶媳妇—<b>尽想好事</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><a class="lemma-album layout-right nslog:10000206" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/2589468/8367d1fcbbe1cdcfb801a0e1?fr=lemma&amp;ct=cover" nslog-type="10000206" style="width:222px;" target="_blank" title="臧金生版猪八戒">

</div>
</a>
猪八戒吃猪肉—<b>自相残杀</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒骑驴—<b>一对牲口</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒结亲—<b>一个喜来一个忧</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒擦粉—<b>遮不了丑</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒咬牙—<b>恨猴</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒看唱本—<b>假斯文</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒的脊背—<b>悟（无）能之背（辈）</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒吃西瓜— <b>独吞</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒嫁妹子—<b>看我就行</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒丢了钉耙—<b>凭什么保师傅</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒下棋—<b>准输</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒走路—<b>左右摇摆</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒摔耙子—<b>不干了</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒啃猪蹄—<b>不知自觉（脚）</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒见高小姐—<b>改换了头面</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒见了白骨精—<b>垂涎三尺</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒拉着西施拜天地—<b>压根不配</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒招亲—<b>凡心难却</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒进了女儿国—<b>不想走了</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒卖炒肝—<b>这是哪道肺</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒的嘴巴 —<b>自我欣赏</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒啃地梨—<b>什么仙人吃什么果</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒吃猪蹄—<b>自残骨肉</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:220px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/0/377adab44aed2e731f22c6588001a18b86d6faff?fr=lemma&amp;ct=single" nslog-type="9317" style="width:220px;height:146px;" target="_blank" title="猪八戒">

</a>
<span class="description">
猪八戒
</span>
</div>猪八戒吃黄连—<b>苦了大嘴的</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒吃人参果—<b>全不知滋味</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">解释：比喻吃东西狼吞虎咽，来不及细尝。也比喻看书做事贪多务得，实则无所收获。 出处：清·<a href="/item/%E5%90%B4%E6%95%AC%E6%A2%93" target="_blank">吴敬梓</a>《<a data-lemmaid="27018" href="/item/%E5%84%92%E6%9E%97%E5%A4%96%E5%8F%B2/27018" target="_blank">儒林外史</a>》第六回：“你这奴才，‘猪八戒吃人参果，全不知滋味’”。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒耍把式—<b>倒打一耙</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒过火焰山—<b>倒把一耙</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒了天拜佛—<b>掸心不稳</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒背媳妇—<b>舍得花力气（或费力不讨好）</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒肖媳妇—<b>心甘情愿</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒想娶媳妇—<b>一厢情愿</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒发眸气—<b>又丑又恶</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒照镜子—<b>自找难堪</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒上城墙—<b>倒打一耙</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒调戏嫦娥—<b>也不掂量掂量自己</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">猪八戒背孙悟空—<b>能人背后有能人</b></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><a class="lemma-album layout-right nslog:10000206" href="/pic/%E7%8C%AA%E5%85%AB%E6%88%92/769/2589467/241f95cad1c8a786499d46286609c93d70cf5064?fr=lemma&amp;ct=cover" nslog-type="10000206" style="width:222px;" target="_blank" title="马德华版猪八戒">
<div class="album-wrap" style="width:220px;height:176px;">
<img alt="马德华版猪八戒" class="picture" src="https://gss0.bdstatic.com/94o3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=6557de0791ef76c6d4d2fc29ad17fdf6/241f95cad1c8a786499d46286609c93d70cf5064.jpg" style="width:220px;height:176px;"/>

猪八戒戴眼镜—<b>冒充大学生</b></div>

<div class="tashuo-author">

<div class="overlay"><img src="https://bkssl.bdimg.com/static/wiki-lemma/widget/lemma_content/mainContent/tashuo/img/overlay_1ccc6d9.png"/></div>
<p class="title">
西游记最深不可测之人，天庭对他提防，其师父连玉帝都畏惧三分
</p></a>
<p class="abstract">
<a href="/tashuo/browse/content?id=229718be515cab3eff26aea8&amp;lemmaId=&amp;fromLemmaModule=pcBottom" target="_blank">
妖族与巫族已经是上古时代的事情了。成立天庭之后，月亮就成了巫族高级首领的聚集地，更是修行地。因为月亮会给这些巫族的修炼者提供神秘的力量。“我代表月亮消灭你”绝非一句空洞的口号哦。</a>
</p>
<div class="tashuo-operator">
<span class="tashuo-publish-date">2017-10-30</span><span class="tashuo-like J-like " data-isvote="0"><i></i><strong class="J-number">491</strong></span>
</div>
</li>
<li class="tashuo-item J-item" data-tashuoid="e1f2a8e89492574ecabbffce">
<div class="tashuo-author">
<a href="/tashuo/authorcenter?authorId=afa769b974bbc541c9cfd727" target="_blank">
<div class="ta-author-area"><span><img src="https://imgsa.baidu.com/baike/pic/item/86d6277f9e2f070841f1b9a8e024b899a801f2a6.jpg"/></span></div>
<div class="ta-author-slogan-area">
<strong>蜗牛看西游</strong>
<span>读西游故事 看社会人生</span>
</div>
<i></i></a>
</div>
<a class="cover" href="/tashuo/browse/content?id=e1f2a8e89492574ecabbffce&amp;lemmaId=&amp;fromLemmaModule=pcBottom" target="_blank">
<img class="cover-img" data-height="479" data-width="640" src="https://imgsa.baidu.com/baike/pic/item/9c16fdfaaf51f3de067058689feef01f3b2979f8.jpg"/>
<div class="overlay"><img src="https://bkssl.bdimg.com/static/wiki-lemma/widget/lemma_content/mainContent/tashuo/img/overlay_1ccc6d9.png"/></div>
<p class="title">
猪八戒为何不愿当净坛使者？如来其实给他挖了一个坑？
</p></a>
<p class="abstract">
<a href="/tashuo/browse/content?id=e1f2a8e89492574ecabbffce&amp;lemmaId=&amp;fromLemmaModule=pcBottom" target="_blank">
如来关于吃的问题，已经承诺了两个人，首先承诺的是自己的舅舅，然后才是八戒。也就是说，八戒即使天天吃，也只能吃大鹏剩下的！</a>
</p>
<div class="tashuo-operator">
<span class="tashuo-publish-date">2017-10-02</span><span class="tashuo-like J-like " data-isvote="0"><i></i><strong class="J-number">361</strong></span>
</div>
</li>
<li class="tashuo-item J-item" data-tashuoid="76f8efb940c1c8cf8ffed6a5">
<div class="tashuo-author">
<a href="/tashuo/authorcenter?authorId=b3e54008a24ed52773648f25" target="_blank">
<div class="ta-author-area"><span><img src="https://imgsa.baidu.com/baike/pic/item/d01373f082025aaf192b6064f3edab64034f1a07.jpg"/></span></div>
<div class="ta-author-slogan-area">
<strong>历史大学堂</strong>
<span>品读书史，历史堂原创出品</span>

<i></i></a>
</div>
<a class="cover" href="/tashuo/browse/content?id=76f8efb940c1c8cf8ffed6a5&amp;lemmaId=&amp;fromLemmaModule=pcBottom" target="_blank">
<img class="cover-img" data-height="396" data-width="640" src="https://imgsa.baidu.com/baike/pic/item/d50735fae6cd7b89579c1fed042442a7d8330eef.jpg"/>
<div class="overlay"><img src="https://bkssl.bdimg.com/static/wiki-lemma/widget/lemma_content/mainContent/tashuo/img/overlay_1ccc6d9.png"/></div>
<p class="title">
西游记中最被轻视的人，看似胆小怕事，关键时刻却多次救了悟空
</p></a>
<p class="abstract">
<a href="/tashuo/browse/content?id=76f8efb940c1c8cf8ffed6a5&amp;lemmaId=&amp;fromLemmaModule=pcBottom" target="_blank">
一部西游记，说起来就是唐僧师徒和妖怪们斗智斗勇史。你赢了你过关，你输了，对不起妖怪要蒸熟了吃唐僧肉，好长生不老。</a>
</p>
<div class="tashuo-operator">
<span class="tashuo-publish-date">2017-10-21</span><span class="tashuo-like J-like " data-isvote="0"><i></i><strong class="J-number">330</strong></span>
</div>
</li>
<li class="tashuo-item J-item" data-tashuoid="aeb9b7bbc2de5c7b3a2720bc">
<div class="tashuo-author">
<a href="/tashuo/authorcenter?authorId=5936ecdc32c5dea02c407a20" target="_blank">
<div class="ta-author-area"><span><img src="https://imgsa.baidu.com/baike/pic/item/bd315c6034a85edf71cb53e340540923dc5475af.jpg"/></span></div>
<div class="ta-author-slogan-area">
<strong>历史百家争鸣</strong>
<span>历史从未如此丰富多彩</span>
</div>
<i></i></a>
</div>
<a class="cover" href="/tashuo/browse/content?id=aeb9b7bbc2de5c7b3a2720bc&amp;lemmaId=&amp;fromLemmaModule=pcBottom" target="_blank">
<img class="cover-img" data-height="413" data-width="720" src="https://imgsa.baidu.com/baike/pic/item/908fa0ec08fa513d87a5dc67366d55fbb2fbd978.jpg"/>
<div class="overlay"><img src="https://bkssl.bdimg.com/static/wiki-lemma/widget/lemma_content/mainContent/tashuo/img/overlay_1ccc6d9.png"/></div>
<p class="title">
唐僧师徒五人谁的结局最好呢？
</p></a>
<p class="abstract">
<a href="/tashuo/browse/content?id=aeb9b7bbc2de5c7b3a2720bc&amp;lemmaId=&amp;fromLemmaModule=pcBottom" target="_blank">
唐僧师徒五人到达西天见到如来佛，除了取到经书之外，最重要的就是封圣，唐僧和孙悟空都成佛了，八戒是净坛使者，而沙僧是金身罗汉，小白龙是八部天龙菩萨，那么对于他们五人来说，到底是不是名副其实的封圣呢？看起来好像孙悟空和唐僧成佛了，结局应该最好，就他们两人成佛了，其他人都没有，但...</a>
</p>
<div class="tashuo-operator">
<span class="tashuo-publish-date">2017-11-13</span><span class="tashuo-like J-like " data-isvote="0"><i></i><strong class="J-number">312</strong></span>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="slider-item">
<ul class="tashuo-list">
<li class="tashuo-item J-item" data-tashuoid="1fc94913511f981d62aa3939">
<div class="tashuo-author">
<a href="/tashuo/authorcenter?authorId=b3e54008a24ed52773648f25" target="_blank">
<div class="ta-author-area"><span><img src="https://imgsa.baidu.com/baike/pic/item/d01373f082025aaf192b6064f3edab64034f1a07.jpg"/></span></div>
<div class="ta-author-slogan-area">
<strong>历史大学堂</strong>
<span>品读书史，历史堂原创出品</span>
</div>
<i></i></a>
</div>
<a class="cover" href="/tashuo/browse/content?id=1fc94913511f981d62aa3939&amp;lemmaId=&amp;fromLemmaModule=pcBottom" target="_blank">
<img class="cover-img" data-height="425" data-width="640" src="https://imgsa.baidu.com/baike/pic/item/279759ee3d6d55fb52e6089e67224f4a20a4dd62.jpg"/>
<div class="overlay"><img src="https://bkssl.bdimg.com/static/wiki-lemma/widget/lemma_content/mainContent/tashuo/img/overlay_1ccc6d9.png"/></div>
<p class="title">
同样都要延寿，为何地上的妖都想吃唐僧肉，而天上的仙却不敢
</p></a>
<p class="abstract">
<a href="/tashuo/browse/content?id=1fc94913511f981d62aa3939&amp;lemmaId=&amp;fromLemmaModule=pcBottom" target="_blank">
寿命无限延长了，可能瞬移的事情也不再是一种传说了。那么我们的须弥世界，可能又会面临着与其他高维世界更复杂的竞争了。</a>
</p>
<div class="tashuo-operator">
<span class="tashuo-publish-date">2017-06-26</span><span class="tashuo-like J-like " data-isvote="0"><i></i><strong class="J-number">293</strong></span>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul></div>
<div class="tashuo-bottom-pager"></div>
</div>
